    { PROPERTIES
      {
        DataItemIndent=1;
        DataItemTable=Table91;
        DataItemTableView=SORTING(User ID);
        DataItemVarName=Sales Approval;
        OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                        IF UserCode = '' THEN
                          ERROR(Text005);
                        LastFieldNo := FIELDNO("User ID");
                        IF WhatToTest <> WhatToTest::All THEN BEGIN
                          IF WhatToTest <> WhatToTest::Sales THEN
                            CurrReport.BREAK;
                        END;
                        SETRANGE("User ID",UserCode);

                        UserTEMP.DELETEALL;
                      END;

        OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                           UserSetup@1000 : Record 91;
                           SalesApprovalAmount@1001 : Integer;
                           ErrorMessage@1002 : Text[200];
                         BEGIN
                           CLEAR(SalesApprovalRoute);
                           OK := FALSE;
                           Status := Text001;
                           Stop := FALSE;
                           Break := FALSE;
                           SalesApprovalAmount := 0;
                           I := 1;
                           TESTFIELD("Approver ID");
                           SalesApprovalRoute[I,1] := "Sales Approval"."User ID";
                           SalesApprovalRoute[I,2] := "Sales Approval"."Approver ID";
                           SalesApprovalRoute[I,3] := FORMAT("Sales Approval"."Sales Amount Approval Limit");
                           SalesApprovalRoute[I,4] := FORMAT("Sales Approval"."Unlimited Sales Approval");
                           SalesApprovalRoute[I,5] := ErrorMessage;
                           SalesApprovalRoute[I,6] := FORMAT(I);
                           SalesApprovalRoute[I,7] := Status;
                           SalesApprovalAmount := "Sales Amount Approval Limit";
                           CLEAR(ErrorMessage);

                           UserTEMP := "Sales Approval";
                           UserTEMP.INSERT;

                           SalesApprovalAmount := "Sales Amount Approval Limit";
                           IF "Unlimited Sales Approval" THEN BEGIN
                             Break := TRUE;
                             ErrorMessage := Text012;
                             Status := Text001;
                             OK := TRUE;
                             CLEAR(ErrorMessage);
                           END;
                           IF NOT Break THEN BEGIN
                             UserSetup.SETRANGE("User ID","Sales Approval"."Approver ID");
                             IF UserSetup.FIND('-') THEN BEGIN
                               REPEAT
                                 UserTEMP := UserSetup;
                                 IF NOT UserTEMP.INSERT THEN BEGIN
                                   ErrorMessage := STRSUBSTNO(Text007,UserSetup."User ID",Text013);
                                   Status := Text002;
                                   Break := TRUE;
                                 END;

                                 I := I + 1;
                                 IF UserSetup."User ID" = '' THEN
                                   UserSetup."User ID" := Text014;
                                 IF UserSetup."Unlimited Sales Approval" THEN BEGIN
                                   Break := TRUE;
                                   ErrorMessage := Text012;
                                   OK := TRUE;
                                   Status := Text001;
                                 END;
                                 IF (UserSetup."Sales Amount Approval Limit" < SalesApprovalAmount) AND NOT
                                    UserSetup."Unlimited Sales Approval" THEN BEGIN
                                   ErrorMessage := STRSUBSTNO(Text006,UserSetup.FIELDCAPTION("Sales Amount Approval Limit"));
                                   Status := Text002;
                                   Break := TRUE;
                                   Stop := TRUE;
                                 END;
                                 SalesApprovalRoute[I,1] := UserSetup."User ID";
                                 SalesApprovalRoute[I,2] := UserSetup."Approver ID";
                                 SalesApprovalRoute[I,3] := FORMAT(UserSetup."Sales Amount Approval Limit");
                                 SalesApprovalRoute[I,4] := FORMAT(UserSetup."Unlimited Sales Approval");
                                 SalesApprovalRoute[I,5] := ErrorMessage;
                                 SalesApprovalRoute[I,6] := FORMAT(I);
                                 SalesApprovalRoute[I,7] := Status;
                                 SalesApprovalAmount := UserSetup."Sales Amount Approval Limit";
                                 IF UserSetup."Unlimited Sales Approval" THEN BEGIN
                                   OK := TRUE;
                                   Break := TRUE;
                                 END;

                                 IF NOT Break THEN BEGIN
                                   UserSetup.SETRANGE("User ID",UserSetup."Approver ID");
                                   IF UserSetup.FIND('-') THEN
                                     UserSetup.SETRANGE("User ID",UserSetup."Approver ID");
                                 END;
                                 IF I = 500 THEN
                                   Break := TRUE;
                               UNTIL Break;
                             END;
                           END;
                         END;

        GroupTotalFields=User ID;
      }

       }
    { PROPERTIES
      {
        DataItemIndent=1;
        DataItemTable=Table91;
        DataItemTableView=SORTING(User ID);
        DataItemVarName=Purchase Approval;
        OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                        IF UserCode = '' THEN
                          ERROR(Text005);
                        IF WhatToTest <> WhatToTest::All THEN BEGIN
                          IF WhatToTest <> WhatToTest::Purchase THEN
                            CurrReport.BREAK;
                        END;
                        SETRANGE("User ID",UserCode);
                        UserTEMP.DELETEALL;
                      END;

        OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                           UserSetup@1002 : Record 91;
                           PurchaseApprovalAmount@1000 : Integer;
                           ErrorMessage@1001 : Text[200];
                         BEGIN
                           CLEAR(SalesApprovalRoute);
                           OK := FALSE;
                           Status := Text001;
                           Stop := FALSE;
                           Break := FALSE;

                           PurchaseApprovalAmount := 0;
                           I := 1;
                           TESTFIELD("Approver ID");
                           SalesApprovalRoute[I,1] := "Purchase Approval"."User ID";
                           SalesApprovalRoute[I,2] := "Purchase Approval"."Approver ID";
                           SalesApprovalRoute[I,3] := FORMAT("Purchase Approval"."Purchase Amount Approval Limit");
                           SalesApprovalRoute[I,4] := FORMAT("Purchase Approval"."Unlimited Purchase Approval");
                           SalesApprovalRoute[I,5] := ErrorMessage;
                           SalesApprovalRoute[I,6] := FORMAT(I);
                           SalesApprovalRoute[I,7] := Status;
                           PurchaseApprovalAmount := "Purchase Amount Approval Limit";
                           CLEAR(ErrorMessage);

                           UserTEMP := "Purchase Approval";
                           UserTEMP.INSERT;

                           PurchaseApprovalAmount := "Purchase Amount Approval Limit";
                           IF "Unlimited Purchase Approval" THEN BEGIN
                             Break := TRUE;
                             ErrorMessage := Text012;
                             Status := Text001;
                             OK := TRUE;
                             CLEAR(ErrorMessage);
                           END;
                           IF NOT Break THEN BEGIN
                             UserSetup.SETRANGE("User ID","Purchase Approval"."Approver ID");
                             IF UserSetup.FIND('-') THEN BEGIN
                               REPEAT
                                 UserTEMP := UserSetup;
                                 IF NOT UserTEMP.INSERT THEN BEGIN
                                   ErrorMessage := STRSUBSTNO(Text007,UserSetup."User ID",Text015);
                                   Status := Text002;
                                   Break := TRUE;
                                 END;
                                 I := I + 1;
                                 IF UserSetup."User ID" = '' THEN
                                   UserSetup."User ID" := Text014;
                                 IF UserSetup."Unlimited Purchase Approval" THEN BEGIN
                                   Break := TRUE;
                                   ErrorMessage := Text012;
                                   OK := TRUE;
                                   Status := Text001;
                                 END;
                                 IF (UserSetup."Purchase Amount Approval Limit" < PurchaseApprovalAmount) AND NOT
                                    UserSetup."Unlimited Purchase Approval" THEN BEGIN
                                   ErrorMessage := STRSUBSTNO(Text006,UserSetup.FIELDCAPTION("Unlimited Purchase Approval"));
                                   Status := Text002;
                                   Break := TRUE;
                                   Stop := TRUE;
                                 END;
                                 SalesApprovalRoute[I,1] := UserSetup."User ID";
                                 SalesApprovalRoute[I,2] := UserSetup."Approver ID";
                                 SalesApprovalRoute[I,3] := FORMAT(UserSetup."Purchase Amount Approval Limit");
                                 SalesApprovalRoute[I,4] := FORMAT(UserSetup."Unlimited Purchase Approval");
                                 SalesApprovalRoute[I,5] := ErrorMessage;
                                 SalesApprovalRoute[I,6] := FORMAT(I);
                                 SalesApprovalRoute[I,7] := Status;
                                 PurchaseApprovalAmount := UserSetup."Purchase Amount Approval Limit";
                                 IF UserSetup."Unlimited Purchase Approval" THEN
                                   Break := TRUE;

                                 IF NOT Break THEN BEGIN
                                   UserSetup.SETRANGE("User ID",UserSetup."Approver ID");
                                   IF UserSetup.FIND('-') THEN
                                     UserSetup.SETRANGE("User ID",UserSetup."Approver ID");
                                 END;
                                 IF I = 500 THEN
                                   Break := TRUE;
                               UNTIL Break;
                             END;
                           END;
                         END;

      }

    { PROPERTIES
      {
        DataItemIndent=1;
        DataItemTable=Table91;
        DataItemTableView=SORTING(User ID);
        DataItemVarName=Request Approval;
        OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                        IF UserCode = '' THEN
                          ERROR(Text005);
                        IF WhatToTest <> WhatToTest::All THEN BEGIN
                          IF WhatToTest <> WhatToTest::Request THEN
                            CurrReport.BREAK;
                        END;
                        SETRANGE("User ID",UserCode);
                        UserTEMP.DELETEALL;
                      END;

        OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                           UserSetup@1002 : Record 91;
                           RequestApprovalAmount@1000 : Integer;
                           ErrorMessage@1001 : Text[200];
                         BEGIN
                           CLEAR(SalesApprovalRoute);
                           OK := FALSE;
                           Status := Text001;
                           Stop := FALSE;
                           Break := FALSE;

                           RequestApprovalAmount := 0;
                           I := 1;
                           TESTFIELD("Approver ID");
                           SalesApprovalRoute[I,1] := "Request Approval"."User ID";
                           SalesApprovalRoute[I,2] := "Request Approval"."Approver ID";
                           SalesApprovalRoute[I,3] := FORMAT("Request Approval"."Request Amount Approval Limit");
                           SalesApprovalRoute[I,4] := FORMAT("Request Approval"."Unlimited Request Approval");
                           SalesApprovalRoute[I,5] := ErrorMessage;
                           SalesApprovalRoute[I,6] := FORMAT(I);
                           SalesApprovalRoute[I,7] := Status;
                           RequestApprovalAmount := "Request Amount Approval Limit";
                           CLEAR(ErrorMessage);

                           UserTEMP := "Request Approval";
                           UserTEMP.INSERT;

                           RequestApprovalAmount := "Request Amount Approval Limit";
                           IF "Unlimited Request Approval" THEN BEGIN
                             Break := TRUE;
                             ErrorMessage := Text012;
                             Status := Text001;
                             OK := TRUE;
                             CLEAR(ErrorMessage);
                           END;
                           IF NOT Break THEN BEGIN
                             UserSetup.SETRANGE("User ID","Request Approval"."Approver ID");
                             IF UserSetup.FIND('-') THEN BEGIN
                               REPEAT
                                 UserTEMP := UserSetup;
                                 IF NOT UserTEMP.INSERT THEN BEGIN
                                   ErrorMessage := STRSUBSTNO(Text007,UserSetup."User ID",Text016);
                                   Status := Text002;
                                   Break := TRUE;
                                 END;
                                 I := I + 1;
                                 IF UserSetup."User ID" = '' THEN
                                   UserSetup."User ID" := Text014;
                                 IF UserSetup."Unlimited Request Approval" THEN BEGIN
                                   Break := TRUE;
                                   ErrorMessage := Text012;
                                   Status := Text001;
                                   OK := TRUE;
                                 END;
                                 IF (UserSetup."Request Amount Approval Limit" < RequestApprovalAmount) AND NOT
                                    UserSetup."Unlimited Request Approval" THEN BEGIN
                                   ErrorMessage := STRSUBSTNO(Text006,UserSetup.FIELDCAPTION("Unlimited Request Approval"));
                                   Status := Text002;
                                   Break := TRUE;
                                   Stop := TRUE;
                                 END;
                                 SalesApprovalRoute[I,1] := UserSetup."User ID";
                                 SalesApprovalRoute[I,2] := UserSetup."Approver ID";
                                 SalesApprovalRoute[I,3] := FORMAT(UserSetup."Request Amount Approval Limit");
                                 SalesApprovalRoute[I,4] := FORMAT(UserSetup."Unlimited Request Approval");
                                 SalesApprovalRoute[I,5] := ErrorMessage;
                                 SalesApprovalRoute[I,6] := FORMAT(I);
                                 SalesApprovalRoute[I,7] := Status;
                                 RequestApprovalAmount := UserSetup."Request Amount Approval Limit";
                                 IF UserSetup."Unlimited Request Approval" THEN
                                   Break := TRUE;

                                 IF NOT Break THEN BEGIN
                                   UserSetup.SETRANGE("User ID",UserSetup."Approver ID");
                                   IF UserSetup.FIND('-') THEN
                                     UserSetup.SETRANGE("User ID",UserSetup."Approver ID");
                                 END;
                                 IF I = 500 THEN
                                   Break := TRUE;
                               UNTIL Break;
                             END;
                           END;
                         END;

      }

    PROCEDURE MakeStatusText@1000000015(ApprovalCaption@1000000000 : Text[250]) : Text[250];
    BEGIN
      IF ISSERVICETIER THEN
        IF OK AND NOT Stop THEN
          EXIT(STRSUBSTNO(Text004,ApprovalCaption))
        ELSE
          EXIT(STRSUBSTNO(Text003,ApprovalCaption));
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
